<li><b>1946</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mervyn_Peake" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Mervyn Peake">Mervyn Peake</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Titus_Groan" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Titus Groan"><a href = vnd.unilang:titus.html>Titus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groan.html>Groan</a></a></i>
<dl><dd>Concurrently <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> Flay'<a href = vnd.unilang:s.html>s</a> visualization <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cleaver.html>cleaver</a></b> falling—the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cleaver.html>cleaver</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:fell.html>fell</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:music.html>music</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> Bahamas</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:type.html>type</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> clave, <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rhythm.html>rhythm</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stick.html>stick</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> concussive <a href = vnd.unilang:musical.html>musical</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:instrument.html>instrument</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:used.html>used</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:traditional.html>traditional</a> Bahamian <a href = vnd.unilang:music.html>music</a>.</li>

***clif.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:clif.html>clif</a> (94562)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klibą</i>. <p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:new.html>New</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:clitoris.html>clitoris</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κλειτορίς</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kleitorís</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***cobweb.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cobweb.html>cobweb</a> (94549)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">copweb</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">coppeweb</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cop.html>cop</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:spider.html>spider</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:web.html>web</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kopwebbe</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:low.html>Low</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">Kobbenwebbe</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Westphalian</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a> Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:an.html>an</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:article.html>article</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:on.html>on</a>:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/cobweb" class="extiw" title="w:cobweb"><a href = vnd.unilang:cobweb.html>cobweb</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/cobweb" class="extiw" title="w:cobweb">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cobweb.html>cobweb</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">cobwebs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spiderweb.html>spiderweb</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:remains.html>remains</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:one.html>one</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:especially.html>especially</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:an.html>an</a> asymmetrical <a href = vnd.unilang:one.html>one</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:that.html>that</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> woven <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:an.html>an</a> irregular <a href = vnd.unilang:pattern.html>pattern</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> threads.
